```markdown
</Broside>

Allowing filers to describe their emotions 'in their own words' resulted in feelings the dashboards could not legally acknowledge.
</Broside>

<Broside type="tip" title="Provisional codes allocated. F17 through F93." icon="hash" id="0114-SOMA-5">

</Broside>

<Broside type="tip" title="Compliantly numb. Collapsed state." icon="minimize-2" id="0114-SOMA-6">

</Broside>

SOMA appealed the existence of too many emotions. Resolution is deferred until humans agree to feel less.
</Broside>
```

```markdown
Attempting to prove a finding does not belong to your team is recorded as defensive behavior, which immediately qualifies as an inherited trait.
</Broside>
<Broside type="tip" title="Sins of the predecessor." icon="users" id="0384-8">
Systemic failures do not vanish when closed; they simply wait in the database until they can be blamed on a completely innocent junior administrator.
</Broside>

<Broside type="tip" title="Genealogy of failure." icon="git-merge" id="0384-9">
Your team is currently on probation because an intern used the wrong font in an apology memo twelve years ago.
</Broside>

<Broside type="tip" title="Appealing the inevitable." icon="shield-off" id="0384-10">
Filing an appeal to remove an inherited defect is the fastest way to prove that your department has inherited the defect of complaining.
</Broside>

```
